xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p>✨ <strong>New</strong> — Introduced in <code><a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="5e24313a1e6a706f">[email&#160;protected]</a></code></p>
</div></div></div>
<p>All Zod schemas can process inputs in both the forward and backward direction:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Forward</strong>: <code>Input</code> to <code>Output</code>
<ul>
<li><code>.parse()</code></li>
<li><code>.decode()</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Backward</strong>: <code>Output</code> to <code>Input</code>
<ul>
<li><code>.encode()</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>In most cases, this is a distinction without a difference. The input and output types are identical, so there&#x27;s no difference between &quot;forward&quot; and &quot;backward&quot;.</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;asdf&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);   </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; &quot;asdf&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;asdf&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; &quot;asdf&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;asdf&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; &quot;asdf&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_9iilubv9fl5b_-trigger-zod-mini" hidden="" id="radix-_R_9iilubv9fl5b_-content-zod-mini" tabindex="0" class="p-4 prose-no-margin [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:-m-4 [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:rounded-none [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:border-none"></div></div>
<p>However, some schema types cause the input and output types to diverge, notably <code>z.codec()</code>. Codecs are a special type of schema that defines a <em>bi-directional transformation</em> between two other schemas.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> stringToDate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">codec</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  z.iso.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">datetime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// input schema: ISO date string</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),          </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// output schema: Date object</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">isoString</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(isoString), </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ISO string → Date</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> date.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toISOString</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),       </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Date → ISO string</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>In these cases, <code>z.decode()</code> and <code>z.encode()</code> behave quite differently.</p>
<div dir="ltr" data-orientation="horizontal" class="flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-xl border bg-fd-card my-4"><div role="tablist" aria-orientation="horizontal" class="flex flex-row items-end gap-4 overflow-x-auto bg-fd-secondary px-4 text-fd-muted-foreground" tabindex="-1" data-orientation="horizontal" style="outline:none"><button type="button" role="tab" aria-selected="true" aria-controls="radix-_R_hiilubv9fl5b_-content-zod" data-state="active" id="radix-_R_hiilubv9fl5b_-trigger-zod" class="whitespace-nowrap border-b border-transparent py-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors hover:text-fd-accent-foreground disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 data-[state=active]:border-fd-primary data-[state=active]:text-fd-primary" tabindex="-1" data-orientation="horizontal" data-radix-collection-item="">Zod</button><button type="button" role="tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="radix-_R_hiilubv9fl5b_-content-zod-mini" disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 data-[state=active]:border-fd-primary data-[state=active]:text-fd-primary" tabindex="-1" data-orientation="horizontal" data-radix-collection-item="">Zod Mini</button></div><div data-state="active" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_hiilubv9fl5b_-trigger-zod" id="radix-_R_hiilubv9fl5b_-content-zod" tabindex="0" class="p-4 prose-no-margin [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:-m-4 [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:rounded-none [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:border-none" style="animation-duration:0s"><figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;2024-01-15T10:30:00.000Z&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; Date</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;2024-01-15T10:30:00.000Z&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">))</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; string</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_hiilubv9fl5b_-trigger-zod-mini" hidden="" id="radix-_R_hiilubv9fl5b_-content-zod-mini" tabindex="0" class="p-4 prose-no-margin [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:-m-4 [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:rounded-none [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:border-none"></div></div>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p><strong>Note</strong> —There&#x27;s nothing special about the directions or terminology here. Instead of <em>encoding</em> with an <code>A -&gt; B</code> codec, you could instead <em>decode</em> with a <code>B -&gt; A</code> codec. The use of the terms &quot;decode&quot; and &quot;encode&quot; is just a convention.</p>
</div></div></div>
<p>This is particularly useful when parsing data at a network boundary. You can share a single Zod schema between your client and server, then use this single schema to convert between a network-friendly format (say, JSON) and a richer JavaScript representation.</p>
<div class="relative "><img alt="Codecs encoding and decoding data across a network boundary" loading="lazy" width="800" height="400" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" class="block dark:hidden" style="color:transparent;height:auto;width:100%" src="/codecs/codecs-network-light.svg"/><img alt="Codecs encoding and decoding data across a network boundary" loading="lazy" width="800" height="400" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" class="hidden dark:block" style="color:transparent;height:auto;width:100%" src="/codecs/codecs-network-dark.svg"/></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="composability"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=composability">Composability</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p><strong>Note</strong> — You can use <code>z.encode()</code> and <code>z.decode()</code> with any schema. It doesn&#x27;t have to be a ZodCodec.</p>
</div></div></div>
<p>Codecs are a schema like any other. You can nest them inside objects, arrays, pipes, etc. There are no rules on where you can use them!</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> payloadSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  startDate: stringToDate </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">payloadSchema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  startDate: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;2024-01-15T10:30:00.000Z&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { startDate: Date }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="type-safe-inputs"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=type-safe-inputs">Type-safe inputs</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>While <code>.parse()</code> and <code>.decode()</code> behave identically at <em>runtime</em>, they have different type signatures. The <code>.parse()</code> method accepts <code>unknown</code> as input, and returns a value that matches the schema&#x27;s inferred <em>output type</em>. By contrast, the <code>z.decode()</code> and <code>z.encode()</code> functions have <em>strongly-typed inputs</em>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">12345</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// no complaints from TypeScript (fails at runtime)</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">12345</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ TypeScript error: Argument of type &#x27;number&#x27; is not assignable to parameter of type &#x27;string&#x27;.</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">12345</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ TypeScript error: Argument of type &#x27;number&#x27; is not assignable to parameter of type &#x27;Date&#x27;.</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Why the difference? Encoding and decoding imply <em>transformation</em>. In many cases, the inputs to these methods are already strongly typed in application code, so z.decode/z.encode accept strongly typed inputs to surface mistakes at compile time.
Here&#x27;s a diagram demonstrating the differences between the type signatures for <code>parse()</code>, <code>decode()</code>, and <code>encode()</code>.</p>
<div class="relative "><img alt="Codec directionality diagram showing bidirectional transformation between input and output schemas" loading="lazy" width="800" height="400" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" class="block dark:hidden" style="color:transparent;height:auto;width:100%" srcSet="/_next/image?url=%2Fcodecs%2Fcodecs-light.png&amp;w=828&amp;q=100 1x, /_next/image?url=%2Fcodecs%2Fcodecs-light.png&amp;w=1920&amp;q=100 2x" src="/_next/image?url=%2Fcodecs%2Fcodecs-light.png&amp;w=1920&amp;q=100"/><img alt="Codec directionality diagram showing bidirectional transformation between input and output schemas" loading="lazy" width="800" height="400" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" class="hidden dark:block" style="color:transparent;height:auto;width:100%" srcSet="/_next/image?url=%2Fcodecs%2Fcodecs-dark.png&amp;w=828&amp;q=100 1x, /_next/image?url=%2Fcodecs%2Fcodecs-dark.png&amp;w=1920&amp;q=100 2x" src="/_next/image?url=%2Fcodecs%2Fcodecs-dark.png&amp;w=1920&amp;q=100"/></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="async-and-safe-variants"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=async-and-safe-variants">Async and safe variants</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>As with <code>.transform()</code> and <code>.refine()</code>, codecs support async transforms.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> asyncCodec</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">codec</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(), z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(), {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(str),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">num</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> num.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toString</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>As with regular <code>parse()</code>, there are &quot;safe&quot; and &quot;async&quot; variants of <code>decode()</code> and <code>encode()</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;2024-01-15T10:30:00.000Z&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; Date</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decodeAsync</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;2024-01-15T10:30:00.000Z&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; Promise&lt;Date&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">safeDecode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;2024-01-15T10:30:00.000Z&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; { success: true, data: Date } | { success: false, error: ZodError }</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">safeDecodeAsync</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;2024-01-15T10:30:00.000Z&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; Promise&lt;{ success: true, data: Date } | { success: false, error: ZodError }&gt;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="how-encoding-works"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=how-encoding-works">How encoding works</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>There are some subtleties to how certain Zod schemas &quot;reverse&quot; their parse behavior.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="codecs"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=codecs">Codecs</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>This one is fairly self-explanatory. Codecs encapsulate a bi-directional transformation between two types. <code>z.decode()</code> triggers the <code>decode</code> transform to convert input into a parsed value, while <code>z.encode()</code> triggers the <code>encode</code> transform to serialize it back.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> stringToDate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">codec</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  z.iso.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">datetime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// input schema: ISO date string</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),          </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// output schema: Date object</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">isoString</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(isoString), </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ISO string → Date</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">    encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> date.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toISOString</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),       </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Date → ISO string</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;2024-01-15T10:30:00.000Z&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; Date</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;2024-01-15&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; string</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="pipes"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=pipes">Pipes</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p><strong>Fun fact</strong> — Codecs are actually implemented internally as <em>subclass</em> of pipes that have been augmented with &quot;interstitial&quot; transform logic.</p>
</div></div></div>
<p>During regular decoding, a <code>ZodPipe&lt;A, B&gt;</code> schema will first parse the data with <code>A</code>, then pass it into <code>B</code>. As you might expect, during encoding, the data is first encoded with <code>B</code>, then passed into <code>A</code>.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="refinements"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=refinements">Refinements</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>All checks (<code>.refine()</code>, <code>.min()</code>, <code>.max()</code>, etc.) are still executed in both directions.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> stringToDate.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">refine</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">((</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> date.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">getFullYear</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">&gt;=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> 2000</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Must be this millennium&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;2000-01-01&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">));</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; Date</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;1999-01-01&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">));</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; ❌ ZodError: [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     &quot;code&quot;: &quot;custom&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     &quot;path&quot;: [],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//     &quot;message&quot;: &quot;Must be this millennium&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//   }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ]</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>To avoid unexpected errors in your custom <code>.refine()</code> logic, Zod performs two &quot;passes&quot; during <code>z.encode()</code>. The first pass ensures the input type conforms to the expected type (no <code>invalid_type</code> errors). If that passes, Zod performs the second pass which executes the refinement logic.</p>
<p>This approach also supports &quot;mutating transforms&quot; like <code>z.string().trim()</code> or <code>z.string().toLowerCase()</code>:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">trim</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;  hello  &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; &quot;hello&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;  hello  &quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; &quot;hello&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="defaults-and-prefaults"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=defaults-and-prefaults">Defaults and prefaults</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Defaults and prefaults are only applied in the &quot;forward&quot; direction.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> stringWithDefault</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringWithDefault.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">undefined</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; &quot;hello&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringWithDefault.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">undefined</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; ZodError: Expected string, received undefined</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>When you attach a default value to a schema, the input becomes optional (<code>| undefined</code>) but the output does not. As such, <code>undefined</code> is not a valid input to <code>z.encode()</code> and defaults/prefaults will not be applied.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="catch"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=catch">Catch</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Similarly, <code>.catch()</code> is only applied in the &quot;forward&quot; direction.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> stringWithCatch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">catch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringWithCatch.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">1234</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; &quot;hello&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringWithCatch.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">1234</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; ZodError: Expected string, received number</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="stringbool"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=stringbool">Stringbool</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p><strong>Note</strong> — <a href="/api#stringbool">Stringbool</a> pre-dates the introduction of codecs in Zod. It has since been internally re-implemented as a codec.</p>
</div></div></div>
<p>The <code>z.stringbool()</code> API converts string values (<code>&quot;true&quot;</code>, <code>&quot;false&quot;</code>, <code>&quot;yes&quot;</code>, <code>&quot;no&quot;</code>, etc.) into <code>boolean</code>. By default, it will convert <code>true</code> to <code>&quot;true&quot;</code> and <code>false</code> to <code>&quot;false&quot;</code> during <code>z.encode()</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> stringbool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span <span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringbool.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;true&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; true</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringbool.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;false&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; false</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringbool.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">true</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);    </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; &quot;true&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">stringbool.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">encode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">false</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);   </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; &quot;false&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>If you specify a custom set of <code>truthy</code> and <code>falsy</code> values, the <em>first element in the array</em> will be used instead.</p>

<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="transforms"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=transforms">Transforms</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>⚠️ — The <code>.transform()</code> API implements a <em>unidirectional</em> transformation. If any <code>.transform()</code> exists anywhere in your schema, attempting a <code>z.encode()</code> operation will throw a <em>runtime error</em> (not a <code>ZodError</code>).</p>

<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="useful-codecs"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=useful-codecs">Useful codecs</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Below are implementations for a bunch of commonly-needed codecs. For the sake of customizability, these are not included as first-class APIs in Zod itself. Instead, you should copy/paste them into your project and modify them as needed.</p>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p><strong>Note</strong> — All of these codec implementations have been tested for correctness.</p>
</div></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="stringtonumber"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=stringtonumber"><code>stringToNumber</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Converts string representations of numbers to JavaScript <code>number</code> type using <code>parseFloat()</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> stringToNumber</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span <p>Converts ISO datetime strings to JavaScript <code>Date</code> objects.</p>

<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="jsonschema"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=jsonschema"><code>json(schema)</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Parses JSON strings into structured data and serializes back to JSON. This generic function accepts an output schema to validate the parsed JSON data.</p>

<p>Converts <code>Uint8Array</code> byte arrays to UTF-8 strings.</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">hexToBytes.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">decode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;48656c6c6f&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);     </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; Uint8Array([72, 101, 108, 108, 111])</span></span>

<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="stringtourl"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=stringtourl"><code>stringToURL</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
